***ophoepelen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ophoepelen.html>ophoepelen</a> (13913)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the late 18th century. Compound of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to roll <a href = vnd.unilang:hoops.html>hoops</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. See <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hoepelen.html>hoepelen</a></i> for more on the meaning ‚Äúto go away‚Äù.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ophoepelen.html>ophoepelen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mildly vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to get <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a>, to go away, to piss off
<ul><li><b>1798</b>, "<a href = vnd.unilang:brief.html>Brief</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> Bonifacius Veredik, <a href = vnd.unilang:aangaande.html>aangaande</a> zyn <a href = vnd.unilang:vriend.html>vriend</a> den <a href = vnd.unilang:burger.html>burger</a> Minutieux, <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> D ****.", <i>Vaderlandsche letteroefeningen</i>, page 410.

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:op.html>op</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">up</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kijken.html>kijken</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to look</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<ol><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">rise</span> (of the sun or moon)

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:oplader.html>oplader</a> (32413)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:opladen.html>opladen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äú</span><span class="mention-gloss">to charge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">‚Äù</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oplader.html>oplader</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oplader.html>opladers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oplader.html>opladertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>charger, a device that <a href = vnd.unilang:charges.html>charges</a> or recharges</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
